FNV PPLIGHTING RENDER-STATE GLOBAL IDENTITY FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Questions:
1. Who writes DAT_0126F99C, and is it the same render-state object/class as DAT_0126F6C8?
2. Does renderer +0x8B8 hold a NiDX9RenderState object with vtable B or A?
3. Do virtual slots +0xC0/+0xCC/+0xDC in E7EA00 and E89250/E892D0 map to E88930/E910A0/E88A20?
4. Can the PPLighting pass-entry resource pointer from E7EA00 be tied to final SetTexture stage ownership?

======================================================================
SLOT IDENTITY HYPOTHESIS TO PROVE OR REJECT
======================================================================
If DAT_0126F6C8 and DAT_0126F99C use candidate vtable B at 0x010F088C:
  +0xC0 maps to E88930 (texture-stage-state setter)
  +0xCC maps to E910A0 (sampler-state setter)
  +0xDC maps to E88A20 (SetTexture)
If they use candidate vtable A at 0x010EF60C:
  +0xC0 maps to E88930 and +0xDC maps to E88A20, but +0xCC does not map to E910A0.
This audit must identify the global writers/vtable constructors before E7EA00 +0xDC can be promoted from candidate route to proven SetTexture route.
